  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% Contributor(s): ______________________________________.')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%-------------------------------------------------------------------')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% File    : exprecs.erl')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% @author  : Ulf Wiger <ulf.wiger@ericsson.com>')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% @end')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% Description :')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% Created : 13 Feb 2006 by Ulf Wiger <ulf.wiger@ericsson.com>')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% Rewritten: Jan-Feb 2010 by Ulf Wiger <ulf.wiger@elang-solutions.com>')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%-------------------------------------------------------------------')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% @doc Parse transform for generating record access functions.')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% <p>This parse transform can be used to reduce compile-time')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% dependencies in large systems.</p>')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% <p>In the old days, before records, Erlang programmers often wrote')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% access functions for tuple data. This was tedious and error-prone.')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% The record syntax made this easier, but since records were implemented')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% fully in the pre-processor, a nasty compile-time dependency was')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% introduced.</p>')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% <p>This module automates the generation of access functions for')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% records. While this method cannot fully replace the utility of')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% pattern matching, it does allow a fair bit of functionality on')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% records without the need for compile-time dependencies.</p>')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% <p>Whenever record definitions need to be exported from a module,')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% inserting a compiler attribute,')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% <code>export_records([RecName|...])</code> causes this transform')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% to lay out access functions for the exported records:</p>')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% As an example, consider the following module:')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% <pre>')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% -module(test_exprecs).')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% -export([f/0]).')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% -compile({parse_transform, exprecs}).')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% -record(r, {a = 0 :: integer(),')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%             b = 0 :: integer(),')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%             c = 0 :: integer()}).')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% -record(s,{a}).')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% -export_records([r,s]).')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% f() -&gt;')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%     {new,'#new-r'([])}.')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% </pre>')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% <pre>')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% -module(test_exprecs).')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% -compile({pt_pp_src,true}).')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% -export([f/0]).')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% -record(r,{a = 0 :: integer(),b = 0 :: integer(),c = 0 :: integer()}).')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% -record(s,{a}).')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% -export_records([r,s]).')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% -export(['#exported_records-'/0,')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%          '#new-'/1,')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%          '#info-'/1,')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%          '#info-'/2,')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%          '#pos-'/2,')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%          '#is_record-'/1,')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%          '#is_record-'/2,')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%          '#get-'/2,')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%          '#set-'/2,')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%          '#fromlist-'/2,')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%          '#new-r'/0,')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%          '#new-r'/1,')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%          '#get-r'/2,')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%          '#set-r'/2,')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%          '#pos-r'/1,')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%          '#fromlist-r'/1,')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%          '#fromlist-r'/2,')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%          '#info-r'/1,')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%          '#new-s'/0,')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%          '#new-s'/1,')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%          '#get-s'/2,')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%          '#set-s'/2,')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%          '#pos-s'/1,')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%          '#fromlist-s'/1,')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%          '#fromlist-s'/2,')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%          '#info-s'/1]).')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% -type '#prop-r'() :: {a, integer()} | {b, integer()} | {c, integer()}.')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% -type '#attr-r'() :: a | b | c.')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% -type '#prop-s'() :: {a, any()}.')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% -type '#attr-s'() :: a.')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% -spec '#exported_records-'() -&gt; [r | s].')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% '#exported_records-'() -&gt;')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%     [r,s].')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% -spec '#new-'(r) -&gt; #r{};')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%              (s) -&gt; #s{}.')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% '#new-'(r) -&gt;')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%     '#new-r'();')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% '#new-'(s) -&gt;')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%     '#new-s'().')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% -spec '#info-'(r) -&gt; [a | b | c];')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%               (s) -&gt; [a].')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% '#info-'(RecName) -&gt;')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%     '#info-'(RecName, fields).')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% -spec '#info-'(r, size) -&gt; 4;')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%               (r, fields) -&gt; [a | b | c];')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%               (s, size) -&gt; 2;')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%               (s, fields) -&gt; [a].')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% '#info-'(r, Info) -&gt;')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%     '#info-r'(Info);')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% '#info-'(s, Info) -&gt;')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%     '#info-s'(Info).')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% -spec '#pos-'(r, a) -&gt; 1;')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%              (r, b) -&gt; 2;')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%              (r, c) -&gt; 3;')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%              (s, a) -&gt; 1.')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% '#pos-'(r, Attr) -&gt;')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%     '#pos-r'(Attr);')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% '#pos-'(s, Attr) -&gt;')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%     '#pos-s'(Attr).')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% -spec '#is_record-'(#r{}) -&gt; true;')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%                    (#s{}) -&gt; true;')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%                    (any()) -&gt; false.')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% '#is_record-'(X) -&gt;')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%     if')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%         is_record(X, r) -&gt;')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%             true;')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%         is_record(X, s) -&gt;')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%             true;')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%         true -&gt;')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%             false')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%     end.')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% -spec '#is_record-'(r, #r{}) -&gt; true;')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%                    (s, #s{}) -&gt; true;')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%                    (any(), any()) -&gt; false.')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% '#is_record-'(s, Rec) when tuple_size(Rec) == 2, element(1, Rec) == s -&gt;')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%     true;')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% '#is_record-'(r, Rec) when tuple_size(Rec) == 4, element(1, Rec) == r -&gt;')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%     true;')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% '#is_record-'(_, _) -&gt;')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%     false.')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% -spec '#get-'(a, #r{}) -&gt; integer();')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%              (b, #r{}) -&gt; integer();')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%              (c, #r{}) -&gt; integer();')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%              (a, #s{}) -&gt; any();')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%              (['#attr-r'()], #r{}) -&gt; [integer()];')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%              (['#attr-s'()], #s{}) -&gt; [any()].')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% '#get-'(Attrs, Rec) when is_record(Rec, r) -&gt;')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%     '#get-r'(Attrs, Rec);')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% '#get-'(Attrs, Rec) when is_record(Rec, s) -&gt;')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%     '#get-s'(Attrs, Rec).')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% -spec '#set-'(['#prop-r'()], #r{}) -&gt; #r{};')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%              (['#prop-s'()], #s{}) -&gt; #s{}.')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% '#set-'(Vals, Rec) when is_record(Rec, r) -&gt;')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%     '#set-r'(Vals, Rec);')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% '#set-'(Vals, Rec) when is_record(Rec, s) -&gt;')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%     '#set-s'(Vals, Rec).')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% -spec '#fromlist-'(['#prop-r'()], #r{}) -&gt; #r{};')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%                   (['#prop-s'()], #s{}) -&gt; #s{}.')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% '#fromlist-'(Vals, Rec) when is_record(Rec, r) -&gt;')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%     '#fromlist-r'(Vals, Rec);')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% '#fromlist-'(Vals, Rec) when is_record(Rec, s) -&gt;')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%     '#fromlist-s'(Vals, Rec).')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% -spec '#new-r'() -&gt; #r{}.')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% '#new-r'() -&gt;')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%     #r{}.')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% -spec '#new-r'(['#prop-r'()]) -&gt; #r{}.')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% '#new-r'(Vals) -&gt;')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%     '#set-r'(Vals, #r{}).')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% -spec '#get-r'(a, #r{}) -&gt; integer();')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%               (b, #r{}) -&gt; integer();')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%               (c, #r{}) -&gt; integer();')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%               (['#attr-r'()], #r{}) -&gt; [integer()].')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% '#get-r'(Attrs, R) when is_list(Attrs) -&gt;')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%     [')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%      '#get-r'(A, R) ||')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%          A &lt;- Attrs')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%     ];')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% '#get-r'(a, R) -&gt;')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%     R#r.a;')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% '#get-r'(b, R) -&gt;')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%     R#r.b;')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% '#get-r'(c, R) -&gt;')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%     R#r.c;')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% '#get-r'(Attr, R) -&gt;')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%     error(bad_record_op, ['#get-r',Attr,R]).')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% -spec '#set-r'(['#prop-r'()], #r{}) -&gt; #r{}.')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% '#set-r'(Vals, Rec) -&gt;')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%     F = fun([], R, _F1) -&gt;')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%                R;')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%            ([{a,V}|T], R, F1) when is_list(T) -&gt;')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%                F1(T, R#r{a = V}, F1);')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%            ([{b,V}|T], R, F1) when is_list(T) -&gt;')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%                F1(T, R#r{b = V}, F1);')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%            ([{c,V}|T], R, F1) when is_list(T) -&gt;')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%                F1(T, R#r{c = V}, F1);')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%            (Vs, R, _) -&gt;')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%                error(bad_record_op, ['#set-r',Vs,R])')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%         end,')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%     F(Vals, Rec, F).')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% -spec '#fromlist-r'(['#prop-r'()]) -&gt; #r{}.')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% '#fromlist-r'(Vals) when is_list(Vals) -&gt;')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%     '#fromlist-r'(Vals, '#new-r'()).')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% -spec '#fromlist-r'(['#prop-r'()], #r{}) -&gt; #r{}.')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% '#fromlist-r'(Vals, Rec) -&gt;')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%     AttrNames = [{a,2},{b,3},{c,4}],')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%     F = fun([], R, _F1) -&gt;')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%                R;')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%            ([{H,Pos}|T], R, F1) when is_list(T) -&gt;')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%                case lists:keyfind(H, 1, Vals) of')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%                    false -&gt;')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%                        F1(T, R, F1);')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%                    {_,Val} -&gt;')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%                        F1(T, setelement(Pos, R, Val), F1)')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%                end')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%         end,')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%     F(AttrNames, Rec, F).')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% -spec '#pos-r'('#attr-r'() | atom()) -&gt; integer().')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% '#pos-r'(a) -&gt;')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%     2;')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% '#pos-r'(b) -&gt;')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%     3;')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% '#pos-r'(c) -&gt;')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%     4;')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% '#pos-r'(A) when is_atom(A) -&gt;')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%     0.')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% -spec '#info-r'(fields) -&gt; [a | b | c];')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%                (size) -&gt; 3.')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% '#info-r'(fields) -&gt;')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%     record_info(fields, r);')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% '#info-r'(size) -&gt;')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%     record_info(size, r).')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% -spec '#new-s'() -&gt; #s{}.')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% '#new-s'() -&gt;')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%     #s{}.')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% -spec '#new-s'(['#prop-s'()]) -&gt; #s{}.')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% '#new-s'(Vals) -&gt;')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%     '#set-s'(Vals, #s{}).')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% -spec '#get-s'(a, #s{}) -&gt; any();')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%               (['#attr-s'()], #s{}) -&gt; [any()].')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% '#get-s'(Attrs, R) when is_list(Attrs) -&gt;')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%     [')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%      '#get-s'(A, R) ||')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%          A &lt;- Attrs')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%     ];')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% '#get-s'(a, R) -&gt;')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%     R#s.a;')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% '#get-s'(Attr, R) -&gt;')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%     error(bad_record_op, ['#get-s',Attr,R]).')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% -spec '#set-s'(['#prop-s'()], #s{}) -&gt; #s{}.')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% '#set-s'(Vals, Rec) -&gt;')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%     F = fun([], R, _F1) -&gt;')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%                R;')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%            ([{a,V}|T], R, F1) when is_list(T) -&gt;')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%                F1(T, R#s{a = V}, F1);')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%            (Vs, R, _) -&gt;')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%                error(bad_record_op, ['#set-s',Vs,R])')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%         end,')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%     F(Vals, Rec, F).')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% -spec '#fromlist-s'(['#prop-s'()]) -&gt; #s{}.')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% '#fromlist-s'(Vals) when is_list(Vals) -&gt;')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%     '#fromlist-s'(Vals, '#new-s'()).')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% -spec '#fromlist-s'(['#prop-s'()], #s{}) -&gt; #s{}.')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% '#fromlist-s'(Vals, Rec) -&gt;')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%     AttrNames = [{a,2}],')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%     F = fun([], R, _F1) -&gt;')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%                R;')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%            ([{H,Pos}|T], R, F1) when is_list(T) -&gt;')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%                case lists:keyfind(H, 1, Vals) of')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%                    false -&gt;')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%                        F1(T, R, F1);')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%                    {_,Val} -&gt;')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%                        F1(T, setelement(Pos, R, Val), F1)')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%                end')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%         end,')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%     F(AttrNames, Rec, F).')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% -spec '#pos-s'('#attr-s'() | atom()) -&gt; integer().')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% '#pos-s'(a) -&gt;')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%     2;')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% '#pos-s'(A) when is_atom(A) -&gt;')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%     0.')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% -spec '#info-s'(fields) -&gt; [a];')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%                (size) -&gt; 1.')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% '#info-s'(fields) -&gt;')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%     record_info(fields, s);')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% '#info-s'(size) -&gt;')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%     record_info(size, s).')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% f() -&gt;')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%     {new,'#new-r'([])}.')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% </pre>')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% It is possible to modify the naming rules of exprecs, through the use')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% of the following attributes (example reflecting the current rules):')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% <pre>')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% -exprecs_prefix(["#", operation, "-"]).')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% -exprecs_fname([prefix, record]).')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% -exprecs_vfname([fname, "__", version]).')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% </pre>')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% The lists must contain strings or any of the following control atoms:')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% <ul>')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% <li>in `exprecs_prefix': `operation'</li>')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% <li>in `exprecs_fname': `operation', `record', `prefix'</li>')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% <li>in `exprecs_vfname': `operation', `record', `prefix', `fname', `version'')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% </li>')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% </ul>')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% Exprecs will substitute the control atoms with the string values of the')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% corresponding items. The result will then be flattened and converted to an')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% atom (a valid function or type name).')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% `operation' is one of:')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% <ul>')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% <li>`new'</li>')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% <li>`get'</li>')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% <li>`set'</li>')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% <li>`fromlist'</li>')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% <li>`info'</li>')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% <li>`pos'</li>')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% <li>`is_record'</li>')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% <li>`convert'</li>')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% <li>`prop'</li>')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% <li>`attr'</li>')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% </ul>')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%%')
  PsiComment(function_doc_comment)('%% @end')
